Products in generalGanesh Swamypillaihttp://www.blogger.com/profile/02656684675082724354noreply@blogger.comBlogger114125tag:blogger.com,1999:blog-7872816081050679724.post-3488386986666302692021-01-28T10:08:00.004+05:302021-01-28T10:12:34.989+05:30What is Project InnerEye from Microsoft Research ?<h1 style="height: 0px; text-align: left;">&nbsp;What is Project InnerEye from Microsoft Research ?<br /><br /></h1><div><br /></div><div><br /></div><div><br /></div><div><br /></div><div>( courtesy: Microsoft Research )</div><div><br /></div><div><span style="font-family: verdana; font-size: medium;">As we saw in&nbsp;</span></div><h1 class="post-title" style="background: 0px 0px rgb(255, 255, 255); border: 0px; color: #333333; font-family: Poppins, sans-serif; font-size: 27px; line-height: 1.5em; margin: 0px 0px 15px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; position: relative; vertical-align: baseline;"><br /></h1><h1 class="post-title" style="background: 0px 0px rgb(255, 255, 255); border: 0px; color: #333333; font-family: Poppins, sans-serif; font-size: 27px; line-height: 1.5em; margin: 0px 0px 15px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; position: relative; vertical-align: baseline;"><a href="https://inspire99.github.io/2021/01/what-are-different-research-fields.html" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">What are the different research fields Microsoft has invested into ?</a></h1><div><span style="font-family: verdana; font-size: medium;">Medical Imaging is one research area within Microsoft.</span></div><div><br /></div><div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;"><a href="https://1.bp.blogspot.com/--246KQanEG0/YBI0jmyhBnI/AAAAAAAAyPI/6bI9bMDzDug_QIm_nwitxK6yGHbFw9laACLcBGAsYHQ/s1082/TEMP.jpg" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img border="0" data-original-height="671" data-original-width="1082" height="396" src="https://1.bp.blogspot.com/--246KQanEG0/YBI0jmyhBnI/AAAAAAAAyPI/6bI9bMDzDug_QIm_nwitxK6yGHbFw9laACLcBGAsYHQ/w640-h396/TEMP.jpg" width="640" /></a></div><br /><div><span style="font-family: georgia; font-size: medium;">What is it?</span></div><div><span style="font-family: verdana; font-size: medium;"><br /></span></div><div><span style="font-family: verdana; font-size: medium;">It is an AI technology - it involves machine learning / deep learning related to computer vision. It involves convolutional neural networks.</span></div><div><span style="font-family: verdana; font-size: medium;">Specifically, it involves image segmentation. Image segmentation, wherein the model is able to segment, where healthy organs are and where tumors are. This is a time saver, for an otherwise long manual process.</span></div><div><span style="font-family: verdana; font-size: medium;"><br /></span></div><div><span style="font-family: verdana; font-size: medium;">What is the input ?</span></div><div><span style="font-family: verdana; font-size: medium;"><br /></span></div><div><span style="font-family: verdana; font-size: medium;">3 dimensional medical images.</span></div><div><span style="font-family: verdana; font-size: medium;"><br /></span></div><div><span style="font-family: verdana; font-size: medium;">What is the goal of this project?</span></div><div><span style="font-family: verdana; font-size: medium;"><br /></span></div><div><span style="font-family: verdana; font-size: medium;">Democratizing medical imaging AI,&nbsp;empower researchers, hospitals, life science organizations, and healthcare providers to build medical imaging AI models using Microsoft Azure.</span></div><div><span style="font-family: verdana; font-size: medium;"><br /></span></div><div><span style="font-family: georgia; font-size: medium;">What was the collaboration in this project ?</span></div><div><span style="font-family: verdana; font-size: medium;"><br /></span></div><div><span style="background-color: white; color: #212b32;"><span style="font-family: verdana; font-size: medium;">It was an eight-year collaboration between Cambridge-based Microsoft Research and Addenbrooke’s.</span></span></div><div><span style="font-family: verdana; font-size: medium;"><br /></span></div><div><span style="font-family: georgia; font-size: medium;">What is the aim of this project ?</span></div><div><span style="font-family: verdana; font-size: medium;"><br /></span></div><div><span style="background-color: white; color: #212b32;"><span style="font-family: verdana; font-size: medium;">Its aim is to save clinicians many hours of time laboriously marking up patient scans prior to radiotherapy.</span></span></div><div><span style="background-color: white; color: #212b32;"><span style="font-family: verdana; font-size: medium;"><br /></span></span></div><div><span style="background-color: white; color: #212b32;"><span style="font-family: verdana; font-size: medium;">What is the healthcare domain impacted by this technology?</span></span></div><div><span style="background-color: white; color: #212b32;"><span style="font-family: verdana; font-size: medium;"><br /></span></span></div><div><span style="background-color: white; color: #212b32;"><span style="font-family: verdana; font-size: medium;">Radiotherapy.</span></span></div><div><span face="Frutiger, Arial, sans-serif" style="background-color: white; color: #212b32; font-size: 18px;">Radiotherapy involves focusing high-intensity radiation beams to damage the DNA of hard cancerous tumours while avoiding surrounding healthy organs. This is a critical tool, with around 40% of successfully treated patients undergoing some form of radiotherapy. The important thing is that, damage to healthy organs should not be done. For this, 3-dimensional images are retrieved ( CT - computed tomography scans ). Then the planning is done, and contouring is done, where tumor and healthy organs are marked by clinicians.</span></div><div><span face="Frutiger, Arial, sans-serif" style="background-color: white; color: #212b32; font-size: 18px;"><br /></span></div><div><span face="Frutiger, Arial, sans-serif" style="background-color: white; color: #212b32; font-size: 18px;">LINAC - linear accelerator - radiation beam machine for cancer radiotherapy</span></div><div><span face="Frutiger, Arial, sans-serif" style="background-color: white; color: #212b32; font-size: 18px;"><br /></span></div><div><div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;"><a href="https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-KS6bQW4plUQ/YBI9r8W0SJI/AAAAAAAAyQc/oZiBOcpY_zQfm9pbLpgDWNdZiamZHvjsACLcBGAsYHQ/s1920/LINAC.png" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img border="0" data-original-height="1080" data-original-width="1920" height="360" src="https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-KS6bQW4plUQ/YBI9r8W0SJI/AAAAAAAAyQc/oZiBOcpY_zQfm9pbLpgDWNdZiamZHvjsACLcBGAsYHQ/w640-h360/LINAC.png" width="640" /></a></div><div><br /></div><div><span style="font-family: verdana; font-size: medium;">Planning software, to retrieve 3 d images of the patient</span></div><br /><div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;"><a href="https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-4Vk5l2JWz4U/YBI9r8755gI/AAAAAAAAyQg/QJ9O0JhNCjIUxA4RWNktT3WhR88u6nnGQCLcBGAsYHQ/s1920/PLANNING.png" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img border="0" data-original-height="1080" data-original-width="1920" height="360" src="https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-4Vk5l2JWz4U/YBI9r8755gI/AAAAAAAAyQg/QJ9O0JhNCjIUxA4RWNktT3WhR88u6nnGQCLcBGAsYHQ/w640-h360/PLANNING.png" width="640" /></a></div><div><br /></div><div><br /></div><div><span style="font-family: verdana; font-size: medium;">Segmentation or contouring - marking healthy organs and tumors</span></div><br /><div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;"><a href="https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-mYg9vw4RONA/YBI9r5-IlgI/AAAAAAAAyQk/L1_m8vXwgOcniJ9C1Ll57tLkAWZc9CgqwCLcBGAsYHQ/s1920/SEGMENTATION.png" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img border="0" data-original-height="1080" data-original-width="1920" height="360" src="https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-mYg9vw4RONA/YBI9r5-IlgI/AAAAAAAAyQk/L1_m8vXwgOcniJ9C1Ll57tLkAWZc9CgqwCLcBGAsYHQ/w640-h360/SEGMENTATION.png" width="640" /></a></div><br /><span face="Frutiger, Arial, sans-serif" style="background-color: white; color: #212b32; font-size: 18px;"><br /></span></div><div><span style="background-color: white; color: #212b32;"><span style="font-family: verdana; font-size: medium;"><br /></span></span></div><div><span style="background-color: white; color: #212b32;"><span style="font-family: verdana; font-size: medium;">What is the impact of this project?</span></span></div><div><span style="background-color: white; color: #212b32;"><span style="font-family: verdana; font-size: medium;"><br /></span></span></div><div><span face="Frutiger, Arial, sans-serif" style="background-color: white; color: #212b32; font-size: 18px;">The waiting times for starting potentially life-saving radiotherapy treatment can be dramatically reduced</span></div><div><span face="Frutiger, Arial, sans-serif" style="background-color: white; color: #212b32; font-size: 18px;"><br /></span></div><div><span face="Frutiger, Arial, sans-serif" style="background-color: white; color: #212b32; font-size: 18px;">What are the advantages brought out by this project ?</span></div><div><span face="Frutiger, Arial, sans-serif" style="background-color: white; color: #212b32; font-size: 18px;"><br /></span></div><div><span face="Frutiger, Arial, sans-serif" style="background-color: white; color: #212b32; font-size: 18px;">Helping people receive treatment faster is incredibly important and will not only improve recovery rates but will save clinicians precious time so they can focus on caring for patients.</span></div><div><span face="Frutiger, Arial, sans-serif" style="background-color: white; color: #212b32; font-size: 18px;"><br /></span></div><div><span face="Frutiger, Arial, sans-serif" style="background-color: white; color: #212b32; font-size: 18px;">How is this project useful to radio oncologists ?</span></div><div><span face="Frutiger, Arial, sans-serif" style="background-color: white; color: #212b32; font-size: 18px;"><br /></span></div><div><span face="Frutiger, Arial, sans-serif" style="background-color: white; color: #212b32; font-size: 18px;">It is saving them time. It’s very good at understanding where tumours and healthy organs are. It’s speeding up the process so that the radio oncologists can concentrate on looking at a patient’s diagnostic images and tailor treatment to them.</span></div><div><span face="Frutiger, Arial, sans-serif" style="background-color: white; color: #212b32; font-size: 18px;"><br /></span></div><div><span face="Frutiger, Arial, sans-serif" style="background-color: white; color: #212b32; font-size: 18px;">Project InnerEye aims to answer the following question:</span></div><div><span face="Frutiger, Arial, sans-serif" style="background-color: white; color: #212b32; font-size: 18px;"><br /></span></div><div><span face="&quot;Guardian TextSans Web&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif" style="color: #333333; font-size: 16px;">Can machine learning models achieve clinically acceptable accuracy in image segmentation tasks in radiotherapy planning and reduce overall contouring time?</span></div><div><span face="&quot;Guardian TextSans Web&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif" style="color: #333333; font-size: 16px;"><br /></span></div><div><span face="&quot;Guardian TextSans Web&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif" style="color: #333333; font-size: 16px;">What are the barriers while doing this research?</span></div><div><span face="&quot;Guardian TextSans Web&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif" style="color: #333333; font-size: 16px;"><br /></span></div><div><span face="&quot;Guardian TextSans Web&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif" style="color: #333333; font-size: 16px;">Generalization. The models are expected to work on unseen data. But, also should scale to work on different cancer types and different body parts.</span></div><div><span face="&quot;Guardian TextSans Web&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif" style="color: #333333; font-size: 16px;"><br /></span></div><div><span face="&quot;Guardian TextSans Web&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif" style="color: #333333; font-size: 16px;">What were the training data ?</span></div><div><span face="&quot;Guardian TextSans Web&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif" style="color: #333333; font-size: 16px;"><br /></span></div><div><span face="&quot;Guardian TextSans Web&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif" style="color: #333333; font-size: 16px;">242 head and neck and 519 pelvic computed tomography scans</span></div><div><span face="&quot;Guardian TextSans Web&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif" style="color: #333333; font-size: 16px;"><br /></span></div><div><div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;"><a href="https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-nUjEQc7VY7g/YBI-SoNnTbI/AAAAAAAAyQw/pu4ZVgqVlHsHHrGgPmcqezRp6y7u77V8wCLcBGAsYHQ/s990/trainingdata.jpg" style="margin-left: 1em; one has to choose machine learning artificial intelligence concepts for internship ?<h1 style="text-align: left;">&nbsp;Why one has to choose machine learning artificial intelligence concepts for internship ?</h1><div><br /></div><div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;"><a href="https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-1OJSZlxhFfY/YA-BqX4vD9I/AAAAAAAAyM4/lgqj4Ix6hQIqOq9B3KOKvV8Q75xn4foSgCLcBGAsYHQ/s1158/temp.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img border="0" data-original-height="601" data-original-width="1158" height="332" src="https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-1OJSZlxhFfY/YA-BqX4vD9I/AAAAAAAAyM4/lgqj4Ix6hQIqOq9B3KOKvV8Q75xn4foSgCLcBGAsYHQ/w640-h332/temp.jpg" width="640" /></a></div><br /><div><br /></div><div><span style="font-family: georgia; font-size: medium;">One main reason why one needs to choose machine learning concepts for their internship is , if you are a data science aspirant. There are lot of companies, dealing with huge data. And with huge data, companies want to derive insights. There are lot of senior engineers who are dealing with huge data, but definitely they want lot of help with many nitty-gritty stuff, which they would want to hand off to junior engineers, so that they can focus on the big picture. This is where the interns come in. It is a win-win situation. Interns get to explore the nitty-gritties and are exposed to real world data. Senior engineers get to focus on big picture orchestration, by offloading work.&nbsp;</span></div><div><br /></div><div><br /></div><div><br /></div><div>This post is dedicated to interns who want to get their hands dirty, during their college days, so that, once they become professionals, they have enough ground, to solve real world problems.</div><div><br /></div><div><span style="font-family: verdana; text-align: center;"><br /></div></div></div><p></p><p>Today, I watched 4 videos. One spoke about When to do ML in cloud. And the second video spoke about who are the customers of machine learning. 3rd video was about Lesson overview of Azure ML workspaces. 4th video was about Azure ML Platform introduction.</p><p>When to do ML in cloud?</p><p><br /></p><p><span style="white-space: pre;"> </span>1. Thinking cloud native from the start</p><p><span style="white-space: pre;"> </span>a. Data Governance - security - some leaked data or privacy concern or ransomware</p><p><span style="white-space: pre;"> </span>b. If you want to leverage new Services as they are developed - betting on the platform - features you are not developing,&nbsp;</p><p><span style="white-space: pre;"> </span>2. Hybrid cloud</p><p><span style="white-space: pre;"> </span>a. Use infrastructure as code - treat physical or cloud resource as entities - Use kubernetes to manage burstable cloud resources</p><p><span style="white-space: pre;"> </span>b. Diversification - specialized hardware in your data center - best of both worlds</p><p><span style="white-space: pre;"> </span>3. Migration strategy</p><p><span style="white-space: pre;"> </span>a. Many companies not on cloud, lift and shift strategy - virtualize it - effective way to migrate to cloud - critical game plan for the transition</p><p><br /></p><p>When not to do ML in the cloud?</p><p><span style="white-space: pre;"> </span>1. Legal or Govt or medical requirements - this might not allow to do ML in cloud</p><p><span style="white-space: pre;"> </span>2. Legacy app - If your app is legacy and does not make sense to migrate to cloud.</p><p><span style="white-space: pre;"> </span>3. If you already have specialized HPC - millions of dollars spent in your data center and the project is running successfully - then it does not make sense to use cloud resources</p><p><br /></p><p><br /></p><p><br /></p><p>Customers of Machine learning</p><p><br /></p><p><span style="white-space: pre;"> </span>1. Stakeholders,</p><p><span style="white-space: pre;"> </span>a. Paying customers -&nbsp;</p><p><span style="white-space: pre;"> </span>b. Free customers - helpful in brand on social media - imp to treat all customers as equal</p><p><span style="white-space: pre;"> </span>c. Vulnerable groups - accelerate existing bias - discriminating against people - really think through issues, they may cancel.&nbsp;</p><p><span style="white-space: pre;"> </span>2. Executives</p><p><span style="white-space: pre;"> </span>a. Looking for ROI - results of what you built</p><p><span style="white-space: pre;"> </span>3. Internal Teams</p><p><span style="white-space: pre;"> </span>a. Need metrics to improve - behaviorial metrics - critical to companies survival</p><p><span style="white-space: pre;"> </span>b. Dogfooding&nbsp; - effective way to test the product</p><p><span style="white-space: pre;"> </span>c. Internal products - sw engg use the products internally</p><p><br /></p><p>In this lesson, I learnt about Why, When and Who about Machine learning in the cloud.</p><p><br /></p><p><br /></p><p>Lesson Overview of Workspaces and Azure ML Studio</p><p><br /></p><p><span style="white-space: pre;"> </span>1. We will be looking at AutoML and Hyperparameter Tuning.</p><p><span style="white-space: pre;"> </span>2. Modern ways of doing machine learning involve leveraging proprietary tools, in order to build models quickly and deploy them to real world seamlessly. In older ways, it would take a long time to build a model, but, using AutoML and hyperparameter tuning, you could build upto 100 or 200 models in a day.&nbsp;</p><p><span style="white-space: pre;"> </span>3. The data scientists can focus on the business problem - defining the problem and asking business questions, instead of focusing on the manual repetitive tasks associated with machine learning - this could be done by leveraging the machine learning ecosystem.</p><p><span style="white-space: pre;"> </span>4. How Azure ML platform allows solving ML problems at scale , leveraging Azure cloud</p><p><span style="white-space: pre;"> </span>5. AutoML system - allows team to scale, automate boring tasks</p><p><span style="white-space: pre;"> </span>6. Managing compute resources - choose correct resources, compute instances - it can run jupyterlab. Compute clusters - for training jobs</p><p><span style="white-space: pre;"> </span>7. Inference clusters - using GPUs - online prediction systems</p><p><span style="white-space: pre;"> </span>8. Attached compute - 3rd party solutions like data bricks&nbsp;</p><p><span style="white-space: pre;"> </span>9. Creating notebooks - Jupyter notebooks - ML jobs in cloud. Jupyterlab - team based workflow. Rstudio in Azure</p><p><span style="white-space: pre;"> </span>10. SSH into the machine.</p><p><br /></p><p>What is Azure ML Platform?</p><p><br /></p><p>Azure Cloud - has scalable on-demand compute</p><p>It has data storage, and connectivity</p><p><br /></p><p>Azure ML Studio is built on top of Azure Cloud</p><p>It offers ML workflow orchestration - manage ML workflow</p><p>Model reg and management - MLOps - control the lineage</p><p>Metrics and monitoring - ability to look at compute/ storage/ training job - works effectively or not</p><p>Model deployment - create inference endpoint and deploy model which can run 24/7.</p><p>Cloud is infinite resource for compute / storage - which can scale, depending on ML job requirements</p><p><br /></p><p>Azure ML Studio - what are the sub components</p><p><br /></p><p>Notebooks - Jupyter NB, Rstudio,</p><p>Azure ML Designer - drag and drop interface - no-code or low-code way to create ML Models</p><p>AutoML UI - new way to include team members - to create ML systems easily</p><p>Data labeling - additional insight to data collected</p><p><br /></p><p>Azure Cloud - physical resources - data centers - power, network, cooling. Virtual resource - software defined network or storage. They are available locally or globally. Backplane connecting data center - high transport connectivity.&nbsp;</p><p><br /></p><p>Azure Cloud Service levels - diff levels of controls</p><p>VMs - Customer managed or IAAS - you can control everything</p><p>Service Fabric - PAAS - For example AutoML</p><p>App Service - PAAS</p><p>Functions - code only or serverless - highest level of abstraction</p><div><br /></div><p><br /></p><p><br /></p><div>Today is 11th Jan 2021, Day 2 of 21, I watched 4 videos of the course, again introductory in nature. For example, what if we suddenly need lot of compute power or huge disk-io.</p><p>What if we need to generate lot of data or consume lot of data? Will laptop be able to do that?</p><p><br /></p><p>Elasticity of cloud would be critical to perform real world machine learning. And that cannot be done with laptop powered machine learning.</p><p>Platform tools provided by cloud are constantly evolving and they provide lot of additional capabilities.</p><p>The constraints - cpu, disk io, gpu hardware - are cloud native resources, which are elastic in nature.</p><p><br /></p><p>The platform tools like data lakes provide infinite storage - Apart from storage, we could also provide secured access to data.</p><p>Machine learning Studio - where you can build a model with azure console.</p><p>Cloud also has capability of devops build systems - devops pipelines - integrated with azure machine learning workflow. For example, when your machine learning model is built, what is the next step - we would need to deploy it as a resource which could be accessed.</p><p>Then there is Serverless technology - azure function integration with prediction endpoint. For example, if there is a prediction, that could be tied to a azure function which could be invoked and perform its job. So, we would not waste resources indefinitely, but just for the execution time, machines would be used.</p><p>Sometimes, we would need specific gpu resources , this is available in cloud, on demand.</p><p>We would also need Specialized hardware which allows us to do cloud native machine learning. Cloud also enables us to perform distributed machine learning, where we can provision 10's or 100's of machines to perform machine learning and orchestrate them.</p><p><br /></p><p></p><p>Elasticity - automatically scale infrastructure resources - storage, compute, disk io - to meet demands of the job</p><div>Today is 10th Jan 2021,&nbsp; Day 1 of 21, I have completed watching 3 videos of this course, very introductory in nature. And you want to derive insights out of this data, probably, you might come into conclusion, by writing queries. As we have data, all we can do is query and find the results.</p><p>For example: Which item was most sold in this month? Which item was most viewed on any particular day? etc etc..</p><p>For these, developers or data analysts can write queries or logical stuff, to back-track from there and derive relationships, so that, they are able to pull unrelated variables together and impact business with this new set of insights. For example, there could be some NetFlix shows focusing on Chess game, suddenly there's a spike of interest in Chess game, people watching chess games on youtube. And nowadays, most of the time, on an average, people spend large amount of their personal time on YouTube or other social media. And all this data is being collected and 'served' and interested parties are able to make decisions.&nbsp;</p><p>So, backtracking from a person's life, people can write queries with the data. 1 Terabyte · 1000 Terabytes = 1 Petabyte · <mark class="highlight-yellow_background" style="-webkit-print-color-adjust: exact; background: rgb(251, 243, 219); box-sizing: border-box;">1000 Petabytes = 1 Exabyte</mark>· 1000 Exabytes = 1 Zettabyte · 1000 Zettabytes = 1 Yottabyte · 1000 Yottabytes = 1 Brontobyte · 1000 Brontobytes = 1 Geopbyte</p><ul class="bulleted-list" id="490de1bc-19fa-47d1-8f74-f85a953827d4" style="-webkit-print-color-adjust: exact; border-radius: 0px; border: none; box-sizing: border-box; break-inside: avoid; margin: 1.5em 0px; padding: 0px; margin-block-start: 0.6em; margin: 0px; padding-inline-start: 1.7em;"><li style="-webkit-print-color-adjust: exact; box-sizing: border-box; list-style: disc; padding-left: 0.1em;">Log pipelines aggregate events by same name, and write as log files on HDFS, incoming HDFS. It does Cleansing, format conversion, time ordered partition.</li></ul><ul class="bulleted-list" id="7982dd82-65e9-4c66-8048-16bc3613aed1" style="-webkit-print-color-adjust: exact; box-sizing: border-box; margin-block-end: 0.6em; margin-block-start: 0.6em; margin: 0px; padding-inline-start: 1.7em;"><li style="-webkit-print-color-adjust: exact; box-sizing: border-box; list-style: disc; padding-left: 0.1em;">Real time cluster - SLA is very high - we do rolling upgrade. It is entry point for log files. It is up for several years.</li></ul><ul class="bulleted-list" id="319a55fb-7e21-4af0-8544-651aa94de874" style="-webkit-print-color-adjust: exact; box-sizing: border-box; margin-block-end: 0.6em; margin-block-start: 0.6em; margin: 0px; padding-inline-start: 1.7em;"><li style="-webkit-print-color-adjust: exact; box-sizing: border-box; list-style: disc; padding-left: 0.1em;">Data is collected as hourly partition. From the incoming HDFS, users would have configured, as to which cluster that dataset needs to be replicated. It can be replicated to production clusters or adhoc clusters. </li></ul><ul class="bulleted-list" id="5cfe0225-0d08-4b4c-b2b6-ff608e66e9c7" style="-webkit-print-color-adjust: exact; box-sizing: border-box; margin-block-end: 0.6em; margin-block-start: 0.6em; margin: 0px; padding-inline-start: 1.7em;"><li style="-webkit-print-color-adjust: exact; box-sizing: border-box; list-style: disc; padding-left: 0.1em;">Once data lands on the clusters, jobs run and generate datasets. These data can be replicated to cold storage or production cluster usecases.</li></ul><ul class="bulleted-list" id="34a1dc6f-c40a-4465-b6f2-e83122ff641c" style="-webkit-print-color-adjust: exact; box-sizing: border-box; margin-block-end: 0.6em; margin-block-start: 0.6em; margin: 0px; padding-inline-start: 1.7em;"><li style="-webkit-print-color-adjust: exact; box-sizing: border-box; list-style: disc; padding-left: 0.1em;">Apart from BATCH ANALYTICS, the log pipeline also streams data at realtime, And Apache Heron is used internally for real time stream processing of data.</li></ul><ul class="bulleted-list" id="61f7b482-53f4-4255-b58d-e9352c9df95d" style="-webkit-print-color-adjust: exact; box-sizing: border-box; margin-block-end: 0.6em; margin-block-start: 0.6em; margin: 0px; padding-inline-start: 1.7em;"><li style="-webkit-print-color-adjust: exact; box-sizing: border-box; list-style: disc; padding-left: 0.1em;">So, everyday, 100s of petabytes of data is crunced by 1000s of jobs every day.</li></ul><p id="c9b185a9-ddb3-4657-9876-b30857beb1aa" style="-webkit-print-color-adjust: exact; box-sizing: border-box; margin-bottom: 0.5em; margin-top: 0.5em;"></p><p id="b78a39fa-a7db-465d-851b-a1f903c56185" style="-webkit-print-color-adjust: exact; box-sizing: border-box; margin-bottom: 0.5em; margin-top: 0.5em;"></p><p id="072d1b90-b849-4f76-a1f2-17b3605010d8" style="-webkit-print-color-adjust: exact; margin: 0px; position: relative;"><p cid="n516" class="md-end-block md-p" mdtype="paragraph" style="box-sizing: border-box; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px 0px 0.5rem; orphans: 4; position: relative; white-space: pre-wrap;"><span class="md-plain" md-inline="plain" style="box-sizing: border-box;">Users should be able to create a post - textual / upload photos/ videos</span></p></li><li cid="n521" class="md-list-item" mdtype="list_item" style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px; position: relative;"><p cid="n519" class="md-end-block md-p" mdtype="paragraph" style="box-sizing: border-box; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px 0px 0.5rem; orphans: 4; position: relative; white-space: pre-wrap;"><span class="md-plain" md-inline="plain" style="box-sizing: border-box;">Users should be able to view a newsfeed</span></p></li><li cid="n524" class="md-list-item" mdtype="list_item" style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px; position: relative;"><p cid="n522" class="md-end-block md-p" mdtype="paragraph" style="box-sizing: border-box; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px 0px 0.5rem; orphans: 4; position: relative; white-space: pre-wrap;"><span class="md-plain" md-inline="plain" style="box-sizing: border-box;">Users should be able to connect with others (follow / friend request etc.)</span></p></li><li cid="n527" class="md-list-item" mdtype="list_item" style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px; position: relative;"><p cid="n525" class="md-end-block md-p" mdtype="paragraph" style="box-sizing: border-box; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px 0px 0.5rem; orphans: 4; position: relative; white-space: pre-wrap;"><span class="md-plain" md-inline="plain" style="box-sizing: border-box;">Users could create their pages, focusing on their personal brand </span></p></li><li cid="n530" class="md-list-item" mdtype="list_item" style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px; position: relative;"><p cid="n528" class="md-end-block md-p" mdtype="paragraph" style="box-sizing: border-box; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px 0px 0.5rem; orphans: 4; position: relative; white-space: pre-wrap;"><span class="md-plain" md-inline="plain" style="box-sizing: border-box;">For all active users, whenever there are new posts created by other users, the system should be able to append to the newsfeed for these active users.</span></p></li><li cid="n546" class="md-list-item" mdtype="list_item" style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px; position: relative;"><p cid="n544" class="md-end-block md-p" mdtype="paragraph" style="box-sizing: border-box; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px 0px 0.5rem; orphans: 4; position: relative; white-space: pre-wrap;"><span class="md-plain" md-inline="plain" style="box-sizing: border-box;">Since the app is going to deal with first time internet users, regional languages should be supported, both in the user interface as well as in the content shared by users, in general.</span></p></li><li cid="n549" class="md-list-item" mdtype="list_item" style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px; position: relative;"><p cid="n547" class="md-end-block md-p" mdtype="paragraph" style="box-sizing: border-box; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px 0px 0.5rem; orphans: 4; position: relative; white-space: pre-wrap;"><span class="md-plain" md-inline="plain" style="box-sizing: border-box;">Users should be able to form groups/ communities and chat / post within the group / community and the interaction activity should be visible near-realtime to other users of the group/ community.</span></p></li><li cid="n556" class="md-list-item" mdtype="list_item" style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px; position: relative;"><p cid="n554" class="md-end-block md-p" mdtype="paragraph" style="box-sizing: border-box; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px 0px 0.5rem; orphans: 4; position: relative; white-space: pre-wrap;"><span class="md-plain" md-inline="plain" style="box-sizing: border-box;">Users should be able to transact from the social network, so integration of a reliable payment system should be present.</span></p></li></ol><p cid="n536" class="md-end-block md-p" mdtype="paragraph" style="box-sizing: border-box; color: #333333; font-family: &quot;open sans&quot;, &quot;clear sans&quot;, &quot;helvetica neue&quot;, helvetica, arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; line-height: inherit; margin: 0.8em 0px; orphans: 4; position: relative; white-space: pre-wrap;"><span class="md-plain" md-inline="plain" style="box-sizing: border-box;">What would be the </span><span class="md-pair-s" md-inline="strong" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">non-functional requirements</strong></span><span class="md-plain" md-inline="plain" style="box-sizing: border-box;"> from this app? (in terms of latency, scalability etc)</span></p><ol cid="n537" class="ol-list" mdtype="list" style="box-sizing: border-box; color: #333333; font-family: &quot;open sans&quot;, &quot;clear sans&quot;, &quot;helvetica neue&quot;, helvetica, arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; margin: 0.8em 0px; padding-left: 30px; position: relative;"><li cid="n539" class="md-list-item" mdtype="list_item" style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px; position: relative;"><p cid="n540" class="md-end-block md-p" mdtype="paragraph" style="box-sizing: border-box; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px 0px 0.5rem; orphans: 4; position: relative; white-space: pre-wrap;"><span class="md-plain" md-inline="plain" style="box-sizing: border-box;">The system should be able to generate the newsfeed for any given active user, within a maximum of 2 seconds</span></p></li><li cid="n543" class="md-list-item" mdtype="list_item" style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px; position: relative;"><p cid="n541" class="md-end-block md-p" mdtype="paragraph" style="box-sizing: border-box; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px 0px 0.5rem; orphans: 4; position: relative; white-space: pre-wrap;"><span class="md-plain" md-inline="plain" style="box-sizing: border-box;">When a user publishes a post, this post should make it to the newsfeed of other users, within a maximum of 5 seconds.</span></p></li></ol><p cid="n561" class="md-end-block md-p" mdtype="paragraph" style="box-sizing: border-box; color: #333333; font-family: &quot;open sans&quot;, &quot;clear sans&quot;, &quot;helvetica neue&quot;, helvetica, arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; line-height: inherit; margin: 0.8em 0px; orphans: 4; position: relative; white-space: pre-wrap;"><span class="md-pair-s" md-inline="strong" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">Capacity considerations</strong></span></p><ol cid="n564" class="ol-list" mdtype="list" style="box-sizing: border-box; color: #333333; font-family: &quot;open sans&quot;, &quot;clear sans&quot;, &quot;helvetica neue&quot;, helvetica, arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; margin: 0.8em 0px; padding-left: 30px; position: relative;"><li cid="n566" class="md-list-item" mdtype="list_item" style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px; position: relative;"><p cid="n567" class="md-end-block md-p" mdtype="paragraph" style="box-sizing: border-box; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px 0px 0.5rem; orphans: 4; position: relative; white-space: pre-wrap;"><span class="md-plain" md-inline="plain" style="box-sizing: border-box;">Storage: Let us assume, that, each user posts some content. And for simplicity sake, let us assume that, each user is posting some content of size 10 KB. </span></p><ol cid="n574" class="ol-list" mdtype="list" style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px; padding-left: 30px; position: relative;"><li cid="n573" class="md-list-item" mdtype="list_item" style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px; position: relative;"><p cid="n571" class="md-end-block md-p" mdtype="paragraph" style="box-sizing: border-box; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px 0px 0.5rem; orphans: 4; position: relative; white-space: pre-wrap;"><span class="md-plain" md-inline="plain" style="box-sizing: border-box;">Let us also, assume that, for each user, average post length in a newsfeed is around 10. So, totaling 10 x 10 KB = 100 KB, for 10 posts.</span></p></li><li cid="n577" class="md-list-item" mdtype="list_item" style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px; position: relative;"><p cid="n575" class="md-end-block md-p" mdtype="paragraph" style="box-sizing: border-box; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px 0px 0.5rem; orphans: 4; position: relative; white-space: pre-wrap;"><span class="md-plain" md-inline="plain" style="box-sizing: border-box;">Let us go one step further and also assume that, for quick fetching purpose, around 100 posts need to be stored in memory, So, totalling 100 x 10 KB = 1000 KB for each user.</span></p></li><li cid="n580" class="md-list-item" mdtype="list_item" style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px; position: relative;"><p cid="n578" class="md-end-block md-p" mdtype="paragraph" style="box-sizing: border-box; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px 0px 0.5rem; orphans: 4; position: relative; white-space: pre-wrap;"><span class="md-plain" md-inline="plain" style="box-sizing: border-box;">Now, there are atleast 4 million active users and for each user 1000 KB is required to be stored in memory, so totalling 1000 KB x 4,000,000 = 1 MB x 4, 000, 000 = 4000 MB x 1000 = 4 GB x 1000 = 4000 GB = 4 TB, so 4 TB memory required to store posts.</span></p></li><li cid="n583" class="md-list-item" mdtype="list_item" style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px; position: relative;"><p cid="n581" class="md-end-block md-p" mdtype="paragraph" style="box-sizing: border-box; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px 0px 0.5rem; orphans: 4; position: relative; white-space: pre-wrap;"><span class="md-plain" md-inline="plain" style="box-sizing: border-box;">If a server can hold 40 GB memory, then backend will require atleast 100 server instances, in order, to maintain top 100 posts in memory for all active users.</span></p></li></ol></li><li cid="n586" class="md-list-item" mdtype="list_item" style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px; position: relative;"><p cid="n587" class="md-end-block md-p" mdtype="paragraph" style="box-sizing: border-box; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px 0px 0.5rem; orphans: 4; position: relative; white-space: pre-wrap;"><span class="md-plain" md-inline="plain" style="box-sizing: border-box;">Traffic: Let us assume that, on an average, one user has 100 friends and follows 50 pages. Remember that, there are atleast 4 million active users. Let us also assume that, on an average, each user is accessing their timeline newsfeed for atleast 5 times a day, so there will be 20 million news feed requests per day , or, approximately 5556 newsfeed requests per second.</span></p></li></ol><h3 cid="n509" class="md-end-block md-heading" mdtype="heading" style="box-sizing: border-box; break-after: avoid-page; break-inside: avoid; color: #333333; cursor: text; font-family: &quot;open sans&quot;, &quot;clear sans&quot;, &quot;helvetica neue&quot;, helvetica, arial, sans-serif; font-size: 1.5em; line-height: 1.43; margin-bottom: 1rem; margin-top: 1rem; orphans: 4; position: relative; white-space: pre-wrap;"><span class="md-pair-s" md-inline="underline" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><u style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span class="md-plain" md-inline="plain" style="box-sizing: border-box;">PART-2</span></u></span><span class="md-plain" md-inline="plain" style="box-sizing: border-box;"> - Architectural Details</span></h3><p cid="n507" class="md-end-block md-p" mdtype="paragraph" style="box-sizing: border-box; box-sizing: inherit; clear: both; color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.8); font-family: medium-content-sans-serif-font, -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Oxygen, Ubuntu, Cantarell, &quot;Open Sans&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, sans-serif; margin: 56px auto 0px;"><div class="fr fs ic" style="box-sizing: inherit; margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto; max-width: 400px;"><div class="im r co ff" style="background-color: #f2f2f2; box-sizing: inherit; margin: auto; position: relative;"><div class="in io r" style="box-sizing: inherit; height: 0px; padding-bottom: 595px;"><img alt="Image for post" class="eh ro s t u dt ai c" height="595" sizes="400px" src="https://miro.medium.com/max/500/0*mTL91aYhb32xIc9v.png" srcset="https://miro.medium.com/max/345/0*mTL91aYhb32xIc9v.png 276w, https://miro.medium.com/max/500/0*mTL91aYhb32xIc9v.png 400w" style="background-color: white; box-sizing: inherit; color: #292929; font-family: medium-content-serif-font, Georgia, Cambria, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, serif; font-size: 21px; letter-spacing: -0.003em; line-height: 32px; margin: 2em 0px -0.46em; word-break: break-word;">Nowadays at many websites (which have an integration with Google’s Human Verification Engine), users are shown some set of images. And users are asked to mark some images which contain ice-cream. If the answers are correct, then the user is human. If the answers are wrong, then the user is a bot -&gt; verified not human.</p><p class="is it bi iu b iv iw ix iy iz ja jb jc jd je jf jg jh ji jj jk jl jm jn jo jp gf cw" data-selectable-paragraph="" id="9f79" style="background-color: white; box-sizing: inherit; color: #292929; font-family: medium-content-serif-font, Georgia, Cambria, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, serif; font-size: 21px; letter-spacing: -0.003em; line-height: 32px; margin: 2em 0px -0.46em; word-break: break-word;">My thoughts on above scenario is the following:</p><p class="is it bi iu b iv iw ix iy iz ja jb jc jd je jf jg jh ji jj jk jl jm jn jo jp gf cw" data-selectable-paragraph="" id="d36d" style="background-color: white; box-sizing: inherit; color: #292929; font-family: medium-content-serif-font, Georgia, Cambria, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, serif; font-size: 21px; letter-spacing: -0.003em; line-height: 32px; margin: 2em 0px -0.46em; word-break: break-word;">The verification process assumes that only humans could clearly identify images containing ice-cream. Let us also assume that these testing images are collected from some database reachable by Google. So, these images are already labelled with correct labels so that verification process could be done.</p><h2 class="jq jr bi bh eu js jt ix ju jv jb jw jx jf jy jz jj ka kb jn kc cw" data-selectable-paragraph="" id="d2b5" style="background-color: white; box-sizing: inherit; color: #292929; font-family: medium-content-sans-serif-font, &quot;Lucida Grande&quot;, &quot;Lucida Sans Unicode&quot;, &quot;Lucida Sans&quot;, Geneva, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 26px; letter-spacing: -0.022em; line-height: 32px; margin: 1.72em 0px -0.31em;"><span class="ax" style="box-sizing: inherit; font-weight: inherit;">HUMANS IDENTIFYING ANOTHER HUMAN</span></h2><p class="is it bi iu b iv kd ix iy iz ke jb jc jd kf jf jg jh kg jj jk jl kh jn jo jp gf cw" data-selectable-paragraph="" id="41f0" style="background-color: white; box-sizing: inherit; color: #292929; font-family: medium-content-serif-font, Georgia, Cambria, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, serif; font-size: 21px; letter-spacing: -0.003em; line-height: 32px; margin: 0.86em 0px -0.46em; word-break: break-word;">So, my question is: Are these labelling done by humans?</p><ul class="" style="background-color: white; box-sizing: inherit; color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.8); font-family: medium-content-sans-serif-font, -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Oxygen, Ubuntu, Cantarell, &quot;Open Sans&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, sans-serif; list-style: none none; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;"><li class="is it bi iu b iv iw ix iy iz ja jb jc jd je jf jg jh ji jj jk jl jm jn jo jp ki kj kk cw" data-selectable-paragraph="" id="2f19" style="box-sizing: inherit; color: #292929; font-family: medium-content-serif-font, Georgia, Cambria, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, serif; font-size: 21px; letter-spacing: -0.003em; line-height: 32px; list-style-type: disc; margin-bottom: -0.46em; margin-left: 30px; margin-top: 2em; padding-left: 0px;">If yes, then we are using a mechanism to identify humans based on classification done by another human. It is almost like making a statement: Only a human could identify another human.</li><li class="is it bi iu b iv kl ix iy iz km jb jc jd kn jf jg jh ko jj jk jl kp jn jo jp ki kj kk cw" data-selectable-paragraph="" id="de74" style="box-sizing: inherit; color: #292929; font-family: medium-content-serif-font, Georgia, Cambria, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, serif; font-size: 21px; letter-spacing: -0.003em; line-height: 32px; list-style-type: disc; margin-bottom: -0.46em; margin-left: 30px; margin-top: 1.05em; padding-left: 0px;">If not, then these labelling is done by some image-labelling algorithm or in other words, a bot/algorithm/machine. Basically a bot is used to identify whether a user is a human or a bot. It is almost like making a statement: A bot could identify another bot.</li></ul><h2 class="jq jr bi bh eu js jt ix ju jv jb jw jx jf jy jz jj ka kb jn kc cw" data-selectable-paragraph="" id="5acc" style="background-color: white; box-sizing: inherit; color: #292929; font-family: medium-content-sans-serif-font, &quot;Lucida Grande&quot;, &quot;Lucida Sans Unicode&quot;, &quot;Lucida Sans&quot;, Geneva, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 26px; letter-spacing: -0.022em; line-height: 32px; margin: 1.72em 0px -0.31em;"><span class="ax" style="box-sizing: inherit; font-weight: inherit;">ARTIFICIAL INTELLIGENT MACHINES IDENTIFYING HUMANS</span></h2><p class="is it bi iu b iv kd ix iy iz ke jb jc jd kf jf jg jh kg jj jk jl kh jn jo jp gf cw" data-selectable-paragraph="" id="08db" style="background-color: white; box-sizing: inherit; color: #292929; font-family: medium-content-serif-font, Georgia, Cambria, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, serif; font-size: 21px; letter-spacing: -0.003em; line-height: 32px; margin: 0.86em 0px -0.46em; word-break: break-word;">If 2nd case is correct, following are more questions:-</p><ul class="" style="background-color: white; box-sizing: inherit; color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.8); font-family: medium-content-sans-serif-font, -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Oxygen, Ubuntu, Cantarell, &quot;Open Sans&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, sans-serif; list-style: none none; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;"><li class="is it bi iu b iv iw ix iy iz ja jb jc jd je jf jg jh ji jj jk jl jm jn jo jp ki kj kk cw" data-selectable-paragraph="" id="c915" style="box-sizing: inherit; color: #292929; font-family: medium-content-serif-font, Georgia, Cambria, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, serif; font-size: 21px; letter-spacing: -0.003em; line-height: 32px; list-style-type: disc; margin-bottom: -0.46em; margin-left: 30px; margin-top: 2em; padding-left: 0px;">Is the verification process valid? We are using a bot to identify a human ( Image labelling done by a bot) To what level of accuracy the images are being labelled is the next question, as currently we have research going on within context of Deep Learning.</li><li class="is it bi iu b iv kl ix iy iz km jb jc jd kn jf jg jh ko jj jk jl kp jn jo jp ki kj kk cw" data-selectable-paragraph="" id="2775" style="box-sizing: inherit; color: #292929; font-family: medium-content-serif-font, Georgia, Cambria, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, serif; font-size: 21px; letter-spacing: -0.003em; line-height: 32px; list-style-type: disc; margin-bottom: -0.46em; margin-left: 30px; margin-top: 1.05em; padding-left: 0px;">We are in a situation where we are having lots of research (with increasing accuracy ) in learning mechanisms which try to learn how humans do. In this situation, giving some set of images to a bot and asking to mark would not be a difficult task either. So, should human verification process</li></ul><h2 class="jq jr bi bh eu js jt ix ju jv jb jw jx jf jy jz jj ka kb jn kc cw" data-selectable-paragraph="" id="2999" style="background-color: white; box-sizing: inherit; line-height: 32px; margin: 1.72em 0px -0.31em;"><span class="ax" style="box-sizing: inherit; font-weight: inherit;">ARTIFICIAL INTELLIGENT MACHINES IDENTIFYING ARTIFICIAL INTELLIGENT MACHINES</span></h2><p class="is it bi iu b iv kd ix iy iz ke jb jc jd kf jf jg jh kg jj jk jl kh jn jo jp gf cw" data-selectable-paragraph="" id="7a2b" style="background-color: white; margin: 0.86em 0px -0.46em; word-break: break-word;">Further thoughts:</p><ul class="" style="background-color: white; box-sizing: inherit; color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.8); font-family: medium-content-sans-serif-font, -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, &quot;Segoe UI&quot;, Roboto, Oxygen, Ubuntu, Cantarell, &quot;Open Sans&quot;, &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, sans-serif; margin-bottom: -0.46em; margin-left: 30px; margin-top: 2em; padding-left: 0px;">We are kind of going down the path of creating robots, intelligent cars which will become more pervasive in life of humans compared to before. As before, these were restricted to industries, research area etc. We might as well reach a scenario where artificial intelligent machines would have to verify another artificial intelligent machine. Basically, what is that capability which is present only with artificial intelligent machines? So that this will be considered as verification process, as we assume now that images can be correctly recognized by humans alone.</li><li class="is it bi iu b iv kl ix iy iz km jb jc jd kn jf jg jh ko jj jk jl kp jn jo jp ki kj kk cw" data-selectable-paragraph="" id="0297" style="box-sizing: inherit; color: #292929; font-family: medium-content-serif-font, Georgia, Cambria, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, serif; font-size: 21px; letter-spacing: -0.003em; line-height: 32px; list-style-type: disc; margin-bottom: -0.46em; margin-left: 30px; margin-top: 1.05em; padding-left: 0px;">Probably, ask them to calculate some largest prime number and actually feed it as the input and this could be validated.</li><li class="is it bi iu b iv kl ix iy iz km jb jc jd kn jf jg jh ko jj jk jl kp jn jo jp ki kj kk cw" data-selectable-paragraph="" id="3557" style="box-sizing: inherit; color: #292929; font-family: medium-content-serif-font, Georgia, Cambria, &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, serif; font-size: 21px; letter-spacing: -0.003em; line-height: 32px; list-style-type: disc; margin-bottom: -0.46em; margin-left: 30px; margin-top: 1.05em; padding-left: 0px;">This could also inspire us to ask questions like whether there are things which humans will not be able to recognize using the senses provided to a human? font-size: 16px; font-weight: 400; line-height: inherit; margin: 0.8em 0px; position: relative;"><span class="md-plain" md-inline="plain" style="box-sizing: border-box;">Firstly, a word about statistics:</span></p><p cid="n1253" class="md-end-block md-p" mdtype="paragraph" style="box-sizing: border-box; daily. (</span><span class="md-meta-i-c md-link" md-inline="link" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><a href="http://www.populationu.com/in/tamil-nadu-population#:~:text=Tamil%20Nadu%20population%20in%202020,the%20capital%20of%20Tamil%20nadu." style="-webkit-user-drag: none; box-sizing: border-box; color: #4183c4; cursor: pointer;"><span class="md-plain" md-inline="plain" style="box-sizing: border-box;">Tamil Nadu population - close to 77 million, by 31st May 2020 </span></a></span><span class="md-plain" md-inline="plain" style="box-sizing: border-box;">). </span></p><p cid="n1089" class="md-end-block md-p" mdtype="paragraph" style="box-sizing: border-box; font-size: 16px; font-weight: 400; line-height: inherit; margin: 0.8em 0px; position: relative;"><span class="md-plain" md-inline="plain" style="box-sizing: border-box;">If someone is interested in source of 75 million DAU - you can refer to </span><span class="md-meta-i-c md-link" md-inline="link" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><a href="https://twitter.com/chriscapossela/status/1255617866935595008" style="-webkit-user-drag: none; box-sizing: border-box; color: #4183c4; cursor: pointer;"><span class="md-plain" md-inline="plain" style="box-sizing: border-box;">below tweet</span></a></span><span class="md-plain" md-inline="plain" style="box-sizing: border-box;"> from Microsoft CMO.</span></p><p cid="n2379" class="md-end-block md-p" mdtype="paragraph" style="box-sizing: border-box; font-size: 16px; font-weight: 400; line-height: inherit; margin: 0.8em 0px; position: relative;"><span class="md-plain" md-inline="plain" style="box-sizing: border-box;">(Ofcourse, we can factor out weekends, assuming that, this figure could drop by almost half, considering that most of the companies have weekends off )</span></p><p cid="n249" class="md-end-block md-p" mdtype="paragraph" style="box-sizing: border-box; font-size: 16px; font-weight: 400; line-height: inherit; margin: 0.8em 0px; position: relative;"><span class="md-plain" md-inline="plain" style="box-sizing: border-box;">As of today ( as I write or as you read ), it would have grown even more.</span></p><p cid="n1186" class="md-end-block md-p" mdtype="paragraph" style="box-sizing: border-box; font-size: 16px; font-weight: 400; line-height: inherit; margin: 0.8em 0px; position: relative;"><span class="md-plain" md-inline="plain" style="box-sizing: border-box;">In the first part of this article - I am sharing my system design perspective/ thoughts. If you are not interested, you can directly skip to the second part of the article which contains architecture details (web-scraped &amp; summarized from internet/ videos ).</span></p></h2><h3 cid="n1189" class="md-end-block md-heading" mdtype="heading" style="box-sizing: border-box; line-height: 1.43; margin-bottom: 1rem; margin-top: 1rem; orphans: 4; position: relative; white-space: pre-wrap;"><span class="md-pair-s" md-inline="strong" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span class="md-pair-s" md-inline="underline" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><u style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span class="md-plain" md-inline="plain" style="box-sizing: border-box;">PART-1</span></u></span></strong></span><span class="md-plain" md-inline="plain" style="box-sizing: border-box;"> - System Design Perspectives</span></h3><h2 cid="n2" class="md-end-block md-heading" mdtype="heading" style="border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(238, 238, 238); box-sizing: border-box; break-after: avoid-page; break-inside: avoid; color: #333333; cursor: text; font-family: &quot;open sans&quot;, &quot;clear sans&quot;, &quot;helvetica neue&quot;, helvetica, arial, sans-serif; ( Similar to Facebook Comments/ Reddit Comments ) No, It is a straight line of chats.</span></p></li><li cid="n9" class="md-list-item" mdtype="list_item" style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px; position: relative;"><p cid="n10" class="md-end-block md-p" mdtype="paragraph" style="box-sizing: border-box; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px 0px 0.5rem; orphans: 4; position: relative; white-space: pre-wrap;"><span class="md-plain" md-inline="plain" style="box-sizing: border-box;">What is UI framework used ? Electron ( I guess, but, now it is React-Native ).</span></p></li><li cid="n11" class="md-list-item" mdtype="list_item" style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px; position: relative;"><p cid="n12" class="md-end-block md-p" mdtype="paragraph" style="box-sizing: border-box; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px 0px 0.5rem; orphans: 4; position: relative; white-space: pre-wrap;"><span class="md-plain" md-inline="plain" style="box-sizing: border-box;">(Most importantly) What are the different Azure Cloud Services which is powering MS Teams?</span></p></li><li cid="n13" class="md-list-item" mdtype="list_item" style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px; position: relative;"><p cid="n14" class="md-end-block md-p" mdtype="paragraph" style="box-sizing: border-box; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px 0px 0.5rem; orphans: 4; position: relative; white-space: pre-wrap;"><span class="md-plain" md-inline="plain" style="box-sizing: border-box;">What are the dependencies in Microsoft Office 365 ? (Office suite online)</span></p><ul cid="n231" class="ul-list" data-mark="-" mdtype="list" style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px; padding-left: 30px; position: relative;"><li cid="n230" class="md-list-item md-focus-container" mdtype="list_item" style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px; position: relative;"><p cid="n228" class="md-end-block md-p md-focus" mdtype="paragraph" style="box-sizing: border-box; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px 0px 0.5rem; orphans: 4; position: relative; white-space: pre-wrap;"><span class="md-plain md-expand" md-inline="plain" style="box-sizing: border-box;">As I noted, Word/ PPT is embeddable in Teams? white-space: pre-wrap;"><span class="md-plain" md-inline="plain" style="box-sizing: border-box;">What if there is a live meeting, amongst multiple participants - assume that the network is up for all participants, but MS Teams backend goes down?</span></p><ol cid="n186" class="ol-list" mdtype="list" style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px; padding-left: 30px; position: relative;"><li cid="n185" class="md-list-item" mdtype="list_item" style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px; position: relative;"><p cid="n183" class="md-end-block md-p" mdtype="paragraph" style="box-sizing: border-box; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px 0px 0.5rem; orphans: 4; position: relative; white-space: pre-wrap;"><span class="md-plain" md-inline="plain" style="box-sizing: border-box;">Teams might be recording the meeting as well. So, we can imagine that Microsoft Video Stream service is being used.</span></p></li></ol></li></ol></li></ol></li><li cid="n158" class="md-list-item" mdtype="list_item" style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px; position: relative;"><p cid="n156" class="md-end-block md-p" mdtype="paragraph" style="box-sizing: border-box; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px 0px 0.5rem; orphans: 4; position: relative; white-space: pre-wrap;"><span class="md-pair-s" md-inline="strong" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">upgrade</strong></span><span class="md-plain" md-inline="plain" style="box-sizing: border-box;"> :</span></p><ol cid="n191" class="ol-list" mdtype="list" style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px; padding-left: 30px; position: relative;"><li cid="n196" class="md-list-item" mdtype="list_item" style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px; position: relative;"><p cid="n197" class="md-end-block md-p" mdtype="paragraph" style="box-sizing: border-box; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px 0px 0.5rem; orphans: 4; position: relative; white-space: pre-wrap;"><span class="md-plain" md-inline="plain" style="box-sizing: border-box;"> How is MS Teams upgrading itself, without affecting the continuous streams of chats/ file uploads/ ongoing meetings.</span></p></li></ol></li><li cid="n148" class="md-list-item" mdtype="list_item" style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px; position: relative;"><p cid="n146" class="md-end-block md-p" mdtype="paragraph" style="box-sizing: border-box; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px 0px 0.5rem; orphans: 4; position: relative; white-space: pre-wrap;"><span class="md-pair-s" md-inline="strong" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">performance</strong></span><span class="md-plain" md-inline="plain" style="box-sizing: border-box;">:</span></p><ol cid="n201" class="ol-list" mdtype="list" style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px; padding-left: 30px; position: relative;"><li cid="n200" class="md-list-item" mdtype="list_item" style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px; position: relative;"><p cid="n198" class="md-end-block md-p" mdtype="paragraph" style="box-sizing: border-box; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px 0px 0.5rem; orphans: 4; position: relative; white-space: pre-wrap;"><span class="md-plain" md-inline="plain" style="box-sizing: border-box;">What is the performance guarantee provided by MS Teams, for example, in terms of latency ? For example, when a user searches for some content - a specific keyword - what is the performance guarantee for this query, at the server side? Here, the delivery aspect depends on the network owned by the organization - connectivity with Microsoft Azure infrastructure. But the query-service aspect depends on the algorithms deployed &amp; running internally within Microsoft infrastructure.</span></p></li></ol></li><li cid="n204" class="md-list-item" mdtype="list_item" style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px; position: relative;"><p cid="n205" class="md-end-block md-p" mdtype="paragraph" style="box-sizing: border-box; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px 0px 0.5rem; orphans: 4; position: relative; white-space: pre-wrap;"><span class="md-pair-s" md-inline="strong" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">availability / SLA</strong></span><span class="md-plain" md-inline="plain" style="box-sizing: border-box;">:</span></p><ol cid="n209" class="ol-list" mdtype="list" style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px; padding-left: 30px; position: relative;"><li cid="n208" class="md-list-item" mdtype="list_item" style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px; position: relative;"><p cid="n206" class="md-end-block md-p" mdtype="paragraph" style="box-sizing: border-box; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px 0px 0.5rem; orphans: 4; position: relative; white-space: pre-wrap;"><span class="md-plain" md-inline="plain" style="box-sizing: border-box;">availability of multiple services powering MS Teams. Here it is safe to assume that, since multiple services are powering MS teams, if one service goes down, it does not make sense if all other services are up and running. Again here, we can also safely assume that, probably the user/ the team - is not audience of all the services simultaneously.</span></p></li></ol></li><li cid="n272" class="md-list-item" mdtype="list_item" style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px; position: relative;"><p cid="n273" class="md-end-block md-p" mdtype="paragraph" style="box-sizing: border-box; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px 0px 0.5rem; orphans: 4; position: relative; white-space: pre-wrap;"><span class="md-pair-s" md-inline="strong" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">reliability</strong></span><span class="md-plain" md-inline="plain" style="box-sizing: border-box;">:</span></p><ol cid="n277" class="ol-list" mdtype="list" style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px; padding-left: 30px; position: relative;"><li cid="n276" class="md-list-item" mdtype="list_item" style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px; position: relative;"><p cid="n274" class="md-end-block md-p" mdtype="paragraph" style="box-sizing: border-box; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px 0px 0.5rem; orphans: 4; position: relative; white-space: pre-wrap;"><span class="md-plain" md-inline="plain" style="box-sizing: border-box;">MS Teams should be highly reliable - in the sense - any uploaded file should never be lost</span></p><ol cid="n281" class="ol-list" mdtype="list" style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px; padding-left: 30px; position: relative;"><li cid="n280" class="md-list-item" mdtype="list_item" style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px; position: relative;"><p cid="n278" class="md-end-block md-p" mdtype="paragraph" style="box-sizing: border-box; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px 0px 0.5rem; orphans: 4; position: relative; white-space: pre-wrap;"><span class="md-plain" md-inline="plain" style="box-sizing: border-box;">I guess , this guarantee is ensured by Onedrive for business</span></p><ol cid="n285" class="ol-list" mdtype="list" style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px; padding-left: 30px; position: relative;"><li cid="n284" class="md-list-item" mdtype="list_item" style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px; position: relative;"><p cid="n282" class="md-end-block md-p" mdtype="paragraph" style="box-sizing: border-box; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px 0px 0.5rem; orphans: 4; position: relative; white-space: pre-wrap;"><span class="md-plain" md-inline="plain" style="box-sizing: border-box;">I am still unsure as to what kind of database/ datastore powers Onedrive - which provides this guarantee</span></p></li></ol></li></ol></li></ol></li></ol></li><li cid="n288" class="md-list-item" mdtype="list_item" style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px; position: relative;"><p cid="n292" class="md-end-block md-p" mdtype="paragraph" style="box-sizing: border-box; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px 0px 0.5rem; orphans: 4; position: relative; white-space: pre-wrap;"><span class="md-pair-s" md-inline="strong" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">Design Considerations</strong></span><span class="md-plain" md-inline="plain" style="box-sizing: border-box;">:</span></p><ol cid="n296" class="ol-list" mdtype="list" style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px; padding-left: 30px; position: relative;"><li cid="n295" class="md-list-item" mdtype="list_item" style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px; position: relative;"><p cid="n293" class="md-end-block md-p" mdtype="paragraph" style="box-sizing: border-box; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px 0px 0.5rem; orphans: 4; position: relative; white-space: pre-wrap;"><span class="md-pair-s" md-inline="strong" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">Read-heavy or Write-heavy</strong></span><span class="md-plain" md-inline="plain" style="box-sizing: border-box;">: If we consider this aspect, MS-teams could be designed to be write-heavy. Probably the number of writes are far greater than the number of reads. Because, users are constantly writing to the channels / teams. More often than not, users generally read the latest posts in the channel. Very rarely, users scroll up the feed - which would require multiple reads from the backend. Here, cache could be considered as an option - why should there be a network latency introduced, when we can store content of the device itself.</span></p></li><li cid="n299" class="md-list-item" mdtype="list_item" style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px; position: relative;"><p cid="n297" class="md-end-block md-p" mdtype="paragraph" style="box-sizing: border-box; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px 0px 0.5rem; orphans: 4; position: relative; white-space: pre-wrap;"><span class="md-pair-s" md-inline="strong" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">Cache</strong></span><span class="md-plain" md-inline="plain" style="box-sizing: border-box;"> : Here, again, we should be able to determine if its a smartphone device or a desktop device. With regard to desktop device, the amount of storage is far greater than amount of storage provided by smartphones. So, appropriate decision could be made. For example, there might be more network latency introduced by MS-teams on smartphone, than MS teams on desktop device.</span></p></li><li cid="n302" class="md-list-item" mdtype="list_item" style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px; position: relative;"><p cid="n300" class="md-end-block md-p" mdtype="paragraph" style="box-sizing: border-box; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px 0px 0.5rem; orphans: 4; position: relative; white-space: pre-wrap;"><span class="md-pair-s" md-inline="strong" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">Synchronization</strong></span><span class="md-plain" md-inline="plain" style="box-sizing: border-box;">: Suppose there is a user who has installed MS teams on smartphone as well as desktop device</span></p></li></ol></li><li cid="n305" class="md-list-item" mdtype="list_item" style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px; position: relative;"><p cid="n306" class="md-end-block md-p" mdtype="paragraph" style="box-sizing: border-box; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px 0px 0.5rem; orphans: 4; position: relative; white-space: pre-wrap;"><span class="md-pair-s" md-inline="strong" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">Capacity Estimation &amp; Constraints</strong></span><span class="md-plain" md-inline="plain" style="box-sizing: border-box;">:</span></p><ol cid="n310" class="ol-list" mdtype="list" style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px; padding-left: 30px; position: relative;"><li cid="n309" class="md-list-item" mdtype="list_item" style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px; position: relative;"><p cid="n307" class="md-end-block md-p" mdtype="paragraph" style="box-sizing: border-box; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px 0px 0.5rem; orphans: 4; position: relative; white-space: pre-wrap;"><span class="md-plain" md-inline="plain" style="box-sizing: border-box;">Let's assume the current no. of users: DAU : 75 million total daily active users. (75,000,000)</span></p></li><li cid="n313" class="md-list-item" mdtype="list_item" style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px; position: relative;"><p cid="n311" class="md-end-block md-p" mdtype="paragraph" style="box-sizing: border-box; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px 0px 0.5rem; orphans: 4; position: relative; white-space: pre-wrap;"><span class="md-plain" md-inline="plain" style="box-sizing: border-box;">Let's also make a fair assumption that, each users posts around 100 text messages () per day. And each message is around 100 bytes. So, 100 x 100 = 10 kb - So, each users contributes around 10 kb.</span></p></li><li cid="n1068" class="md-list-item" mdtype="list_item" style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px; position: relative;"><p cid="n1066" class="md-end-block md-p" mdtype="paragraph" style="box-sizing: border-box; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px 0px 0.5rem; orphans: 4; position: relative; white-space: pre-wrap;"><span class="md-plain" md-inline="plain" style="box-sizing: border-box;">Overall, 75 million DAU, will contribute around for text messages alone - </span></p><ol cid="n1073" class="ol-list" mdtype="list" style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px; padding-left: 30px; position: relative;"><li cid="n1072" class="md-list-item" mdtype="list_item" style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px; position: relative;"><p cid="n1070" class="md-end-block md-p" mdtype="paragraph" style="box-sizing: border-box; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px 0px 0.5rem; orphans: 4; position: relative; white-space: pre-wrap;"><span class="md-plain" md-inline="plain" style="box-sizing: border-box;">75,000,000 x 10 kb = 750 megabytes per day ( actually this is very less, this can fit within most pendrives - my assumption is not realistic, but let's continue with this unfair assumption 😊 . Definitely, in terms of enterprise-cloud-thinking - this is not an average enterprise workload - the amount of computing &amp; storage required, inorder to run a workload might vary from usecase to usecase. food for thought - what are the compute-intensive workloads in cloud and what are the storage-intensive workloads in cloud )</span></p></li></ol></li><li cid="n1078" class="md-list-item" mdtype="list_item" style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px; position: relative;"><p cid="n1080" class="md-end-block md-p" mdtype="paragraph" style="box-sizing: border-box; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px 0px 0.5rem; orphans: 4; position: relative; white-space: pre-wrap;"><span class="md-plain" md-inline="plain" style="box-sizing: border-box;">So, total space required for text messages per day, for all 75 million DAU, amounts to just 750 MB.</span></p></li><li cid="n1084" class="md-list-item" mdtype="list_item" style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px; position: relative;"><p cid="n1082" class="md-end-block md-p" mdtype="paragraph" style="box-sizing: border-box; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px 0px 0.5rem; orphans: 4; position: relative; white-space: pre-wrap;"><span class="md-plain" md-inline="plain" style="box-sizing: border-box;">Total space required for 1 day of text messages from all 75 million DAU is 75M * 10 KB = 750 MB.</span></p></li><li cid="n1087" class="md-list-item" mdtype="list_item" style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px; position: relative;"><p cid="n1085" class="md-end-block md-p" mdtype="paragraph" style="box-sizing: border-box; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px 0px 0.5rem; orphans: 4; position: relative; white-space: pre-wrap;"><span class="md-plain" md-inline="plain" style="box-sizing: border-box;">Total space required for 5 years = 750 MB x 5 YEARS x 365 DAYS = 13,68,750 MB or approx 1369 GB. or approx 1.4 TB.</span></p><ol cid="n1098" class="ol-list" mdtype="list" style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px; padding-left: 30px; position: relative;"><li cid="n1097" class="md-list-item" mdtype="list_item" style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px; position: relative;"><p cid="n1095" class="md-end-block md-p" mdtype="paragraph" style="box-sizing: border-box; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px 0px 0.5rem; orphans: 4; position: relative; white-space: pre-wrap;"><span class="md-plain" md-inline="plain" style="box-sizing: border-box;">This can easily fit in hard-disks and with regard to cloud storage offered by Microsoft infrastructure, it is absolutely minimal. ( food for thought: What is the overall storage offered by Microsoft Cloud infrastructure ? )</span></p></li><li cid="n1164" class="md-list-item" mdtype="list_item" style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px; position: relative;"><p cid="n1162" class="md-end-block md-p" mdtype="paragraph" style="box-sizing: border-box; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px 0px 0.5rem; orphans: 4; position: relative; white-space: pre-wrap;"><span class="md-plain" md-inline="plain" style="box-sizing: border-box;">(food for thought: What if we also factor in - audio / video (streamed content) - how much storage would be required approximately?)</span></p></li><li cid="n1161" class="md-list-item" mdtype="list_item" style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px; position: relative;"><p cid="n1159" class="md-end-block md-p" mdtype="paragraph" style="box-sizing: border-box; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px 0px 0.5rem; orphans: 4; position: relative; white-space: pre-wrap;"><span class="md-plain" md-inline="plain" style="box-sizing: border-box;">(</span><span class="md-pair-s" md-inline="strong" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span class="md-pair-s" md-inline="em" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">Assumption !!!, not a fact</em></span></strong></span><span class="md-plain" md-inline="plain" style="box-sizing: border-box;">) If we consider below table related to conversion of bytes for disk storage, probably Microsoft Cloud Storage should hold atleast 1000 petabytes overall. (for 5 years, storing text messages)</span></p><ol cid="n1119" class="ol-list" mdtype="list" style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px; padding-left: 30px; position: relative;"><li cid="n1118" class="md-list-item" mdtype="list_item" style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px; position: relative;"><p cid="n1116" class="md-end-block md-p" mdtype="paragraph" style="box-sizing: border-box; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px 0px 0.5rem; orphans: 4; position: relative; white-space: pre-wrap;"><span class="md-plain" md-inline="plain" style="box-sizing: border-box;">The fair assumption is that, the average organization would require around 1.4 terabytes.</span></p></li><li cid="n1149" class="md-list-item" mdtype="list_item" style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px; position: relative;"><p cid="n1147" class="md-end-block md-p" mdtype="paragraph" style="box-sizing: border-box; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px 0px 0.5rem; orphans: 4; position: relative; white-space: pre-wrap;"><span class="md-plain" md-inline="plain" style="box-sizing: border-box;">As of March 19, 2019, there were 500,000 organizations. So, 500,000 x 1.4 TB = 700,000 TB = 700 PB ~ 1000 PB</span></p></li></ol></li></ol></li></ol></li></ol></h2><h5 cid="n1106" class="md-end-block md-heading" mdtype="heading" style="box-sizing: border-box; break-after: avoid-page; break-inside: avoid; cursor: text; font-size: 1em; line-height: 1.4; margin-bottom: 1rem; margin-top: 0px; orphans: 4; position: relative; white-space: pre-wrap;"><span class="md-plain" md-inline="plain" style="box-sizing: border-box;">Disk Storage (thanks to </span><span class="md-link md-pair-s" md-inline="url" style="box-sizing: border-box; word-break: break-all;"><a href="https://pradeepedwin.wordpress.com/mb-gb-tb-pb-eb-zb-yb-bb/" style="-webkit-user-drag: none; box-sizing: border-box; color: #4183c4; cursor:
