md-heading" mdtype="heading" style="border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(238, 238, 238); box-sizing: border-box; break-after: avoid-page; break-inside: avoid; color: #333333; cursor: text; font-family: &quot;open sans&quot;, &quot;clear sans&quot;, &quot;helvetica neue&quot;, helvetica, arial, sans-serif; font-size: 1.75em; line-height: 1.225; margin-bottom: 1rem; margin-top: 1rem; orphans: 4; padding-bottom: 0.3em; position: relative; white-space: pre-wrap;"><ol cid="n136" class="ol-list" mdtype="list" style="box-sizing: border-box; font-size: 16px; font-weight: 400; margin: 0.8em 0px; orphans: 2; padding-left: 30px; position: relative; white-space: normal;"><li cid="n305" class="md-list-item" mdtype="list_item" style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px; position: relative;"><ol cid="n310" class="ol-list" mdtype="list" style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px; padding-left: 30px; position: relative;"><li cid="n1087" class="md-list-item" mdtype="list_item" style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px; position: relative;"><ol cid="n1098" class="ol-list" mdtype="list" style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px; padding-left: 30px; position: relative;"><li cid="n1161" class="md-list-item" mdtype="list_item" style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px; position: relative;"><ol cid="n1119" class="ol-list" mdtype="list" style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px; padding-left: 30px; position: relative;"><li cid="n1104" class="md-list-item" mdtype="list_item" style="box-sizing: border-box; margin: 0px; position: relative;"><p cid="n1107" class="md-end-block md-p" mdtype="paragraph" style="box-sizing: border-box; line-height: inherit; margin: 0.5rem 0px; orphans: 4; position: relative; white-space: pre-wrap;"><span class="md-plain" md-inline="plain" style="box-sizing: border-box;">· 1 Bit = Binary Digit</span><span class="md-softbreak" md-inline="softbreak" style="box-sizing: border-box;"></span><span class="md-plain" md-inline="plain" style="box-sizing: border-box;">· 8 Bits = 1 Byte</span><span class="md-softbreak" md-inline="softbreak" style="box-sizing: border-box;"></span><span class="md-plain" md-inline="plain" style="box-sizing: border-box;">· 1000 Bytes = 1 Kilobyte</span><span class="md-softbreak" md-inline="softbreak" style="box-sizing: border-box;"></span><span class="md-plain" md-inline="plain" style="box-sizing: border-box;">· 1000 Kilobytes = 1 Megabyte</span><span class="md-softbreak" md-inline="softbreak" style="box-sizing: border-box;"></span><span class="md-plain" md-inline="plain" style="box-sizing: border-box;">· 1000 Megabytes = 1 Gigabyte</span><span class="md-softbreak" md-inline="softbreak" style="box-sizing: border-box;"></span><span class="md-plain" md-inline="plain" style="box-sizing: border-box;">· 1000 Gigabytes = 1 Terabyte</span><span class="md-softbreak" md-inline="softbreak" style="box-sizing: border-box;"></span><span class="md-plain" md-inline="plain" style="box-sizing: border-box;">· 1000 Terabytes = 1 Petabyte</span><span class="md-softbreak" md-inline="softbreak" style="box-sizing: border-box;"></span><span class="md-plain" md-inline="plain" style="box-sizing: border-box;">· 1000 Petabytes = 1 Exabyte</span><span class="md-softbreak" md-inline="softbreak" style="box-sizing: border-box;"></span><span class="md-plain" md-inline="plain" style="box-sizing: border-box;">· 1000 Exabytes = 1 Zettabyte</span><span class="md-softbreak" md-inline="softbreak" style="box-sizing: border-box;"></span><span class="md-plain" md-inline="plain" style="box-sizing: border-box;">· 1000 Zettabytes = 1 Yottabyte</span><span class="md-softbreak" md-inline="softbreak" style="box-sizing: border-box;"></span><span class="md-plain" md-inline="plain" style="box-sizing: border-box;">· 1000 Yottabytes = 1 Brontobyte</span><span class="md-softbreak" md-inline="softbreak" style="box-sizing: border-box;"></span><span class="md-plain" md-inline="plain" style="box-sizing: border-box;">· 1000 Brontobytes = 1 Geopbyte</span></p></li></ol></li></ol></li></ol></li></ol><p cid="n1112" class="md-end-block md-p" mdtype="paragraph" style="box-sizing: border-box; font-size: 16px; font-weight: 400; line-height: inherit; margin: 0.8em 0px; position: relative;"></p><p cid="n1142" class="md-end-block md-p" mdtype="paragraph" style="box-sizing: border-box; font-size: 16px; font-weight: 400; line-height: inherit; margin: 0.8em 0px; position: relative;"><span class="md-pair-s" md-inline="strong" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong Files belonging to </span></p><p cid="n1593" class="md-end-block md-p" mdtype="paragraph" style="box-sizing: border-box; font-size: 16px; font-weight: 400; line-height: inherit; margin: 0.8em 0px; position: relative;"><span class="md-plain" md-inline="plain" style="box-sizing: border-box;">Teams can have many channels.
